/*8. Create tables with its columns according to your normalization (0.125) .
i. If you are using Oracle 11g: Create sequences for every primary key.
ii. If you are using Oracle 12c: Use identity columns.
b. Create primary and foreign keys. */

/***********************************************************************************************
**********************************************************************************************/

CREATE TABLE TypesAircraft(
	Type_AircraftId NUMBER GENERATED ALWAYS AS IDENTITY,
	Description varchar2(255) NOT NULL,
	CodeType varchar2(255) NOT NULL,
	QuantitySeatsBusiness int NOT NULL,
	QuantitySeatsEconomy int NOT NULL,
  CONSTRAINT PK_TypesAircraft PRIMARY KEY(Type_AircraftId));
  
  
 CREATE TABLE Aircrafts(
	AircraftId NUMBER GENERATED ALWAYS AS IDENTITY,
	Registration varchar2(50) NOT NULL,
	Serial_Number varchar2(50) NOT NULL,
	Age int NOT NULL,
	Type_AircraftId int NOT NULL,
 CONSTRAINT PK_Aircrafts PRIMARY KEY (AircraftId),
 CONSTRAINT FK_Type_Aircraft
  FOREIGN KEY (Type_AircraftId)
  REFERENCES TypesAircraft (Type_AircraftId)) ;
    
    
    
  CREATE TABLE TypesAircrew(
	TypeAircrewId NUMBER GENERATED ALWAYS AS IDENTITY,
	Description varchar2(50) NOT NULL,
 CONSTRAINT PK_TypeAircrew PRIMARY KEY(TypeAircrewId));
 

 CREATE TABLE StatusCrews(
	StatusCrewId NUMBER GENERATED ALWAYS AS IDENTITY,
	Description varchar2(50) NOT NULL,
 CONSTRAINT PK_StatusCrews PRIMARY KEY(StatusCrewId));
 

 CREATE TABLE Aircrews(
 AircrewId NUMBER GENERATED ALWAYS AS IDENTITY,
 TypeAircrewId INT NOT NULL,
 FirstName varchar2(50) NOT NULL,
 LastName varchar2(50) NOT NULL,
 Gender varchar2(10) NOT NULL,
 DateOfBirth Date Not Null,
 Seniority varchar2(10) NOT NULL,
 DateLastTraining date,
 Address varchar2(50) NOT NULL,
 Email varchar2(100) NOT NULL,
 CellPhone varchar2(15) NOT NULL,
 HoursBreakTime int,
 StatusCrewId int Not null,
 CurrentLocation varchar2(50)  NULL,
 CONSTRAINT PK_Aircrews PRIMARY KEY(AircrewId),
  CONSTRAINT FK_TypeAircrew
  FOREIGN KEY (TypeAircrewId)
  REFERENCES TypesAircrew (TypeAircrewId),
  CONSTRAINT FK_StatusCrews
  FOREIGN KEY (StatusCrewId)
  REFERENCES StatusCrews (StatusCrewId)
 );

 
 
 CREATE TABLE TypesLicense(
	TypeLicenseId NUMBER GENERATED ALWAYS AS IDENTITY,
	Description varchar2(50) NOT NULL,
 CONSTRAINT PK_TypesLicense PRIMARY KEY(TypeLicenseId));
 
  
 CREATE TABLE PilotsDetail(
	PilotDetailId NUMBER GENERATED ALWAYS AS IDENTITY,
	AircrewId int NOT NULL,
	LevelEnglish varchar2(50) NOT NULL,
	AmountAccumulatedFlightHours int NOT NULL,
	TypeLicenseId int NOT NULL,
	Position varchar2(50) NOT NULL,
 CONSTRAINT PK_PilotsDetail PRIMARY KEY(PilotDetailId),
 CONSTRAINT FK_Aircrews
  FOREIGN KEY (AircrewId)
  REFERENCES Aircrews (AircrewId),
  CONSTRAINT FK_TypesLicense
  FOREIGN KEY (TypeLicenseId)
  REFERENCES TypesLicense (TypeLicenseId));
  

 CREATE TABLE Countries(
	CountryId NUMBER GENERATED ALWAYS AS IDENTITY,
	Description varchar2(50) NOT NULL,
 CONSTRAINT PK_Countries PRIMARY KEY(CountryId));
 
 CREATE TABLE Cities(
	CityId NUMBER GENERATED ALWAYS AS IDENTITY,
	Description varchar2(50) NOT NULL,
	CountryId int NOT NULL,
 CONSTRAINT PK_Cities PRIMARY KEY(CityId),
 CONSTRAINT FK_Countries
  FOREIGN KEY (CountryId)
  REFERENCES Countries (CountryId));
 
 
 CREATE TABLE DocumentTypes(
	DocumentTypeId NUMBER GENERATED ALWAYS AS IDENTITY,
	Description varchar2(50) NULL,
 CONSTRAINT PK_DocumentTypes PRIMARY KEY(DocumentTypeId));
 
 CREATE TABLE Airports(
	AirportId NUMBER GENERATED ALWAYS AS IDENTITY,
	CityId int NOT NULL,
	Name varchar2(50) NOT NULL,
	Latitude varchar2(50) NOT NULL,
	Altitude varchar2(50) NOT NULL,
	Abbreviation varchar2(50) NOT NULL,
 CONSTRAINT PK_Airports PRIMARY KEY(AirportId),
 CONSTRAINT FK_Cities
  FOREIGN KEY (CityId)
  REFERENCES Cities (CityId));
  
 
CREATE TABLE Routes(
	RouteId NUMBER GENERATED ALWAYS AS IDENTITY,
	AirportDepartureId int NOT NULL,
	AirportArrivalId int NOT NULL,
	Distance int NOT NULL,
	FlightNumber varchar2(50) NOT NULL,
	WeeklyFrecuency int NOT NULL,
	QuantityAverageHours int NOT NULL,
 CONSTRAINT PK_Routes PRIMARY KEY(RouteId),
 CONSTRAINT FK_AirportsDeparture
  FOREIGN KEY (AirportDepartureId)
  REFERENCES Airports (AirportId),
  CONSTRAINT FK_AirportsArrival
  FOREIGN KEY (AirportArrivalId)
  REFERENCES Airports (AirportId));
  
  CREATE TABLE LogsFlights(
	LogFlightId NUMBER GENERATED ALWAYS AS IDENTITY,
	Tstamp Int NOT NULL,
	UTC_Time timestamp NOT NULL,
	Latitude varchar2(50) NOT NULL,
	Length varchar2(50) NOT NULL,
	Altitude int NOT NULL,
	Speed int NOT NULL,
	Direction varchar2(50) NOT NULL,
 CONSTRAINT PK_LogsFlights PRIMARY KEY(LogFlightId));
 
 CREATE TABLE RoutesCrewsRequired(
	CrewRequiredId NUMBER GENERATED ALWAYS AS IDENTITY,
	TypeAircrewId int NOT NULL,
	Quantity int NOT NULL,
	RouteId int NOT NULL,
 CONSTRAINT PK_RoutesCrewsRequired PRIMARY KEY(CrewRequiredId),
 CONSTRAINT FK_Routes
  FOREIGN KEY (RouteId)
  REFERENCES Routes (RouteId),
  CONSTRAINT FK_TypeAircrew_RoutesCrewsRequired
  FOREIGN KEY (TypeAircrewId)
  REFERENCES TypesAircrew (TypeAircrewId));
  
  
  CREATE TABLE FlightsConfirmed(
	FlightConfirmId NUMBER GENERATED ALWAYS AS IDENTITY,
	HourEstimateDeparture varchar(15) NOT NULL,
	HourEstimateArrival varchar(15) NOT NULL,
	RealDepartureTime varchar(15) NOT NULL,
	RealArrivalTime varchar(15) NOT NULL,
	RealDuration int NOT NULL,
	AircraftId int NOT NULL,
	PassengerAmount int NOT NULL,
	LogFlightId int NOT NULL,
 CONSTRAINT PK_FlightsConfirmed PRIMARY KEY(FlightConfirmId),
 CONSTRAINT FK_LogsFlights
  FOREIGN KEY (LogFlightId)
  REFERENCES LogsFlights (LogFlightId),
  CONSTRAINT FK_Aircrafts
  FOREIGN KEY (AircraftId)
  REFERENCES Aircrafts (AircraftId));
  
 CREATE TABLE RoutesProgramming(
	RouteProgrammingId NUMBER GENERATED ALWAYS AS IDENTITY,
	RouteId int not NULL,
	DateTimeProgramming timestamp,
 CONSTRAINT PK_RoutesProgramming PRIMARY KEY(RouteProgrammingId),
 CONSTRAINT FK_Routes_Programming
  FOREIGN KEY (RouteId)
  REFERENCES Routes (RouteId));
  
 CREATE TABLE Passengers(
	PassegerId NUMBER GENERATED ALWAYS AS IDENTITY,
	FirstName varchar2(50) NOT NULL,
	LastName varchar2(50) NOT NULL,
	IdentificationNumber varchar2(50) NOT NULL,
	DocumentTypeId int NOT NULL,
	NumberConfirmationChekin varchar2(50) NOT NULL,
	EmergencyContact varchar2(50) NOT NULL,
	CityEmergencyContactIdId int NOT NULL,
	EmailEmergencyContact varchar2(100) NOT NULL,
	EmergencyContactPhoneNumber varchar2(50) NOT NULL,
 CONSTRAINT PK_Passengers PRIMARY KEY(PassegerId),
 CONSTRAINT FK_DocumentTypes
  FOREIGN KEY (DocumentTypeId)
  REFERENCES  DocumentTypes(DocumentTypeId),
  CONSTRAINT FK_Cities_Passengers
  FOREIGN KEY (CityEmergencyContactIdId)
  REFERENCES Cities (CityId) );
  
  
  CREATE TABLE FlightsDetailsCrews(
	FlightDetailCrewId int NOT NULL,
	AircrewId int NOT NULL,
	FlightConfirmId int NOT NULL,
 CONSTRAINT PK_FlightsDetailsCrews PRIMARY KEY(FlightDetailCrewId),
CONSTRAINT FK_Aircrews_Flights
  FOREIGN KEY (AircrewId)
  REFERENCES Aircrews (AircrewId),
  CONSTRAINT FK_FlightsConfirmed
  FOREIGN KEY (FlightConfirmId)
  REFERENCES FlightsConfirmed (FlightConfirmId));

**********************************************************************************************/
